<li>Values and behaviors are affected. Adolescents may attempt to behave more as adults, resolving problems in a responsible manner and making decisions bearing in mind the possible consequences</li>
<li>Increased interest in everyday recreational activities</li>
<li>Increase in mood swings as they seek attention and want to belong and be appreciated</li>
<li>Increased role identification and role modeling.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="reasons-for-focusing-on-adolescents-and-youths-reproductive-health">Reasons for focusing on adolescents and youths Reproductive health<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#reasons-for-focusing-on-adolescents-and-youths-reproductive-health" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>Adolescents and youths RH problems are compounded by many myths, misconceptions and misinformation.</li>
<li>They have different needs because of their physical and psychological stages.</li>
<li>They are more involved in unsafe abortions (for females).</li>
<li>Adolescents and youth are neglected as a group by the health system.</li>
<li>They have different cognitive abilities and skills, which requires different counseling approaches and more time.</li>
</ol>
<p>Reproductive health Lecture notes. Rugendo.M.M @2018 Kabarnet KMTC</p>
<ol start="6">
<li>They tend to be less well-informed and require more information</li>
<li>Conflicts between cultural or parental expectations and adolescents' emerging values present serious challenges for young people.</li>
<li>Using substances or drugs for the first time typically occurs during adolescence.</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="reasons-why-adolescents-and-youths-require-specialized-reproductive-health-services">Reasons why adolescents and youths require specialized Reproductive Health services<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#reasons-why-adolescents-and-youths-require-specialized-reproductive-health-services" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>The specific biological and psychological needs of adolescents.</li>
<li>High risk of STIs, HIV and pregnancy.</li>
<li>Disproportionately high risk of sexual abuse and violence.</li>
<li>Importance of behavior related risks that are responsive to education and counseling.</li>
<li>Opportune age/stage to learn good health practices.</li>
<li>Severities of consequences from lack of reproductive health care.</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="reproductive-health-problems-faced-by-adolescents-and-youth">Reproductive Health problems faced by adolescents and youth<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#reproductive-health-problems-faced-by-adolescents-and-youth" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>a) Early and unprotected sexual intercourses.
b) Female genital cutting
c) Menstrual problems
d) Multiple sexual partners
e) Early and forced marriages
f) Teenage pregnancy and child birth
g) Unsafe abortions
h) Lack of access to RH services and information unmet need for FP
i) Susceptibility to STIs
j) Gender based violence/sexual abuse
k) Drug and substance abuse</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="reproductive-health-needs-amongst-adolescents">Reproductive Health Needs amongst Adolescents<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#reproductive-health-needs-amongst-adolescents" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Information on sexuality and reproductive health</li>
<li>Access to family planning services and provision of effective methods</li>
<li>Prenatal and post abortion care, irrespective of the age or marital status</li>
<li>Safe delivery, preferably in a hospital with facilities for all eventualities</li>
<li>Treatment of unsafe abortions, which should be discouraged, but in the event of any occurrence, post abortion care should be given to save lives</li>
<li>Diagnosis and treatment of sexually transmitted diseases</li>
<li>Protection from sexual abuse. Cases of sexual offenders should be reported to the authorities so that appropriate action can be taken</li>
<li>Culturally appropriate guidance and counselling and or mental health services</li>
<li>Education in negotiating skills to help them make informed choices and accept the consequences of their actions</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="reproductive-health-rights-of-adolescents-and-youth">Reproductive Health rights of adolescents and youth<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#reproductive-health-rights-of-adolescents-and-youth" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>The right to good reproductive health.</li>
<li>The right to decide freely and responsibly on all aspects of one's sexuality.</li>
<li>The right to information and education about sexual and reproductive health so that good decisions can be made about relationships and having children</li>
<li>The right to own, control, and protect one's own body.</li>
</ol>
<p>Reproductive health Lecture notes. Rugendo.M.M @2018 Kabarnet KMTC</p>
<ol start="5">
<li>The right to be free of discrimination, coercion, and violence in one's sexual decisions and sexual life.</li>
<li>The right to expect and demand equality, full consent, and mutual respect in sexual relationships.</li>
<li>The right to quality and affordable reproductive health care regardless of sex, creed, color, marital status, or location.</li>
<li>The right to privacy and confidentiality when dealing with health workers and doctors.</li>
<li>The right to be treated with dignity, courtesy, attentiveness, and respect.</li>
<li>The right to express views on the services offered.</li>
<li>The right to gender equality and equity.</li>
<li>The right to receive reproductive health services for as long as needed.</li>
<li>The right to feel comfortable when receiving services.</li>
<li>The right to choose freely one's life/sexual partners.</li>
<li>The right to celibacy.</li>
<li>The right to refuse marriage.</li>
<li>The right to say no to sex within marriage.</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="barriers-to-adolescents-and-youth-reproductive-health-services">Barriers to adolescents and youth Reproductive Health services<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#barriers-to-adolescents-and-youth-reproductive-health-services" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="a-staff-barriers">A. Staff barriers:-<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#a-staff-barriers" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>Negative attitude toward young people</li>
<li>Lack of training on how to handle young people</li>
<li>Ignorance of the policy is on provision of ASRH services to youth</li>
<li>Personal, religious, and cultural biases among staff</li>
<li>Lack of confidentiality</li>
<li>Lack of privacy</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="b-facility-barriers">B. Facility barriers:-<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#b-facility-barriers" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>Not designed to cater for youth (Inappropriate opening hours, long waiting time)</li>
<li>Lack of privacy</li>
<li>Lack of youth friendly corners</li>
<li>Personal, religious, and cultural biases among staff</li>
<li>Cost of RH services</li>
<li>Lack of Availability of RH services</li>
<li>Long waiting time</li>
<li>Shortage of staff</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="c-socio-cultural-barriers">C. Socio-cultural barriers:-<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#c-socio-cultural-barriers" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>Lack/inadequate information about youth friendly services among community members</li>
<li>Community beliefs, attitudes and misconceptions</li>
<li>Community cultural and religious beliefs</li>
<li>Level of education</li>
<li>Political environment</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="d-personal-adolescent-s-youth-s-barriers">D. Personal/Adolescent's/Youth's barriers:-<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#d-personal-adolescent-s-youth-s-barriers" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>Being embarrassed</li>
<li>Medical procedures (blood tests, pelvic exam)</li>
<li>Non-friendly service providers</li>
</ul>
<p>Reproductive health Lecture notes. Rugendo.M.M @2018 Kabarnet KMTC</p>
<p>&gt; Negative perceived notions towards service providers
&gt; Service provider's attitudes to SRH problems
&gt; Stigma associated with sexual activity and sexual health problems
&gt; Discussing ARH problems with adults</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="adolescent-and-youths-vulnerabilities">Adolescent and youths vulnerabilities<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#adolescent-and-youths-vulnerabilities" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Adolescent and youth vulnerabilities can be classified as follows:</p>
<p>A. Physical vulnerabilities
B. Emotional vulnerabilities
C. Socio-economic vulnerabilities.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="physical-vulnerabilities">Physical vulnerabilities<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#physical-vulnerabilities" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Physical vulnerabilities may include:-</li>
<li>Poor nutrition and inadequate diet</li>
<li>Poor eating habit</li>
<li>Poor health in infancy and childhood</li>
<li>Repeated and untreated infections</li>
<li>Cultural and traditional practices eg. FGM, forced marriage</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="emotional-vulnerabilities">Emotional vulnerabilities<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#emotional-vulnerabilities" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Emotion vulnerabilities may include:-</li>
<li>Adolescents often lack assertiveness and good communication skills, thereby rendering them unable to articulate their needs and withstand pressure or coercion from their peers or adults.</li>
<li>Sexual and physical abuse</li>
<li>Adolescents may feel pressure to conform to stereotypical gender roles.</li>
<li>Young people may lack the maturity to make good, rational decisions.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="socio-economic-vulnerabilities">Socio-economic vulnerabilities.<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#socio-economic-vulnerabilities" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Socio-economic vulnerabilities may include:-</li>
<li>Little access to money and meaningful employment</li>
<li>Poverty and economic hardships</li>
<li>Gender discrimination</li>
<li>Early marriages</li>
<li>Drugs and substance abuse</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="psychosocial-and-behavioral-concerns-of-adolescents">Psychosocial and behavioral concerns of adolescents<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#psychosocial-and-behavioral-concerns-of-adolescents" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>They include: -</p>
<ul>
<li>Gender roles</li>
<li>Peer Relationships/Peer Pressure</li>
<li>Relationships with Parents/Other Adults</li>
<li>Self-Esteem</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="gender-roles">Gender roles<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#gender-roles" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Gender roles are masculine or feminine behaviors expressed according to cultural or social customs and norms.</li>
</ul>
<p>Reproductive health Lecture notes. Rugendo.M.M @2018 Kabarnet KMTC</p>
<p>&gt; Boys achieve more autonomy, mobility, and power, whereas girls tend to get fewer of these privileges and opportunities.
&gt; Boys’ power relative to girls’ translates into dominance in sexual decision-making and expression, often leaving girls unable to fully assert their preferences and rights and to protect their health.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="peer-relationships-peer-pressure">Peer Relationships/Peer Pressure<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#peer-relationships-peer-pressure" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>&gt; Adolescents develop very close relationships with their peers, conforming to language, dress, and customs. This helps them feel secure and gives them a sense of belonging to a large group.
&gt; Given the significance of peer influence, this power can sway adolescents toward greater or lesser risk-taking.
&gt; Peer pressure, combined with gender inequities within a sexual relationship, can mean that males have undue power to dictate sexual decisions to females.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="relationships-with-parents-other-adults">Relationships with Parents/Other Adults<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#relationships-with-parents-other-adults" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>&gt; During adolescence, relationships with parents become more conflicted as the young person tests limits and moves toward greater independence.
&gt; At the same time, parents have significant influence over, and responsibility for, adolescent children.
&gt; Providers are encouraged to promote parent-child communication during this period</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="self-esteem">Self-Esteem<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#self-esteem" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>&gt; Self-esteem is the ability to feel confidence in, and respect for, oneself. It is a feeling of personal competence and self-worth.
&gt; Self-esteem plays a key role in a young person’s sense of how well s/he can deal with life’s options and challenges.
&gt; Specifically for reproductive health, self-esteem influences how young people make judgments about relationships, sex, and sexual responsibility.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="important-life-skills-for-adolescents-and-youths">Important life skills for adolescents and youths<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#important-life-skills-for-adolescents-and-youths" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>&gt; Adolescents need skills to:
&gt; - Help clarify their needs and rights.
&gt; - Express themselves effectively.
&gt; - Decide upon a course of action.</p>
<p>&gt; Life skills are essential component of dealing with youth reproductive issues
&gt; Life skills are abilities or psychological competences that help the individual to deal or cope effectively with the challenges of everyday life.
&gt; They help young people identify goals and build good and healthy futures.
&gt; The acquired abilities are practiced, mastered and perfected to become skills.
&gt; Life skills can be categorized into three:-
&gt; 1) Skills for dealing and coping with oneself</p>
<p>Reproductive health Lecture notes. Rugendo.M.M @2018 Kabarnet KMTC</p>
<ol start="2">
<li>Skills for dealing and coping with others</li>
<li>Skills for making effective decisions</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Skills for dealing and coping with oneself include: -</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Self-awareness</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Self esteem</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Coping with emotions</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Coping with stress</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Goal setting</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Time management</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Skills for dealing and coping with others include: -</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Interpersonal relationships</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Friendship formation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Conflict resolution</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Empathy</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Effective communication</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Resisting peer pressure / assertiveness</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Negotiation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Skills for making effective decisions include: -</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Critical thinking</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Creative thinking</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Decision making</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Problem solving</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Employment/ economic empowerment</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Socialization and Education</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Two life skills will be discussed in details. Students ensure that they have read and understood other types of life skills.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="decision-making">Decision Making<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#decision-making" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>A decision is a choice that we make between two or more possible courses of action</li>
<li>As young people grow, they make decisions some of which will affect them for the rest of their lives.</li>
<li>The most important parts of decision making is predicting outcomes or understanding the consequences of a choice.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="steps-in-decision-making">Steps in decision making<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#steps-in-decision-making" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>Identifying the problem, situation, or issue that is calling for a decision.</li>
<li>Getting more information if you have questions about the situation.</li>
<li>Thinking about the possible consequences or outcomes of each course of action.</li>
<li>Thinking about your personal and family values, and which courses of action are consistent with these values.</li>
<li>Thinking about the ways in which your decision may affect other people.</li>
<li>Choosing the decision that seems most appropriate based on your knowledge, values, morals, religious upbringing, and present and future goals.</li>
</ol>
<p>Reproductive health Lecture notes. Rugendo.M.M @2018 Kabarnet KMTC</p>
<ol start="7">
<li>Re-thinking the decision and how you feel about it – whether you feel that you carefully considered all the alternatives and feel comfortable with the choice you have made.</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Another way you can look at decision making is the use of acronym “DECIDE” Where:-</li>
<li>D-Describe the problem in your own words</li>
<li>E-Explore the available options</li>
<li>C-Choose the option that best fits you</li>
<li>I-Identify the advantages and disadvantages of the option you have chosen</li>
<li>D-Do it if the advantages outweigh the disadvantages</li>
<li>E-Evaluate whether your option is working. If not go back to the first “E”</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="f992b1e4">Three “Cs” for decision making<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#f992b1e4" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>CHALLENGE</li>
<li>CHOICES</li>
<li>CONSEQUENCES</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>CHALLENGE-Describe the CHALLENGE (or decision) you have.</li>
<li>CHOICES-List at least three CHOICES you have</li>
<li>CONSEQUENCES-Consider the positive and negative CONSEQUENCES of each choice.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="goal-setting">Goal setting<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#goal-setting" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>A goal is an achievement and accomplishment towards which our efforts are directed.</li>
<li>Goals give young people something to look forward to.</li>
<li>Goals should be specific, practical, and have a deadline.</li>
<li>Goals should be realistic, manageable and achievable.</li>
<li>Achieving a goal makes it easier and creates confidence among young people to move to other, greater goals.</li>
<li>Thinking about the expected benefits can be motivating.</li>
<li>To help achieve a goal, it is helpful to have a plan with steps that are needed to achieve the goal, and also think about possible difficulties and how they can be overcome.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="questions-to-ask-in-the-goal-setting-process">Questions to ask in the goal setting process.<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#questions-to-ask-in-the-goal-setting-process" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>When do you want to accomplish this goal?</li>
<li>If you reach this goal, in what ways is it going to help you?</li>
<li>What are the steps that you will have to take to reach your goal?</li>
<li>What are the things that might prevent you from achieving your goals?</li>
<li>What actions can you take to overcome these difficulties?</li>
</ul>
<p>Reproductive health Lecture notes. Rugendo.M.M @2018 Kabarnet KMTC</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="youth-friendly-services">Youth friendly services<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#youth-friendly-services" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>YFS are services that are accessible, acceptable, affordable and appropriate for adolescents/youth.</li>
<li>They are in the right place at the right price (free where necessary) and delivered in the right style to be acceptable by young people.</li>
<li>In the right place, at the right price and delivered in the right style to be acceptable to young people.</li>
<li>Effective safe and affordable.</li>
<li>Meet the individual needs of young people who return when they need to and recommend these services to friends.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="rationale-of-guidelines-of-youth-friendly-services">Rationale of Guidelines of Youth Friendly Services<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#rationale-of-guidelines-of-youth-friendly-services" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Services previously offered to young people have been fragmented and varied from one institution to another.</li>
<li>Guidelines aim at harmonising the provision of the services to the beneficiaries.</li>
<li>They provide for a minimum package for services to be considered youth friendly,</li>
<li>Ensures national uniformity of provision of YFS.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="barriers-to-provision-of-yfs">Barriers to provision of YFS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#barriers-to-provision-of-yfs" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Barriers to YFS can be classified into:</li>
<li>a) Staff/health care provider’s barriers</li>
<li>b) Health facility barriers</li>
<li>c) Socio-cultural barriers</li>
<li>d) Adolescent barriers</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="67f7a8d2">Staff/health care providers’ barriers:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#67f7a8d2" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Negative attitude toward young people</li>
<li>Lack of training on how to handle young people</li>
<li>Ignorance of the policy is on provision of ASRH services to youth</li>
<li>Personal, religious, and cultural biases among staff</li>
<li>Lack of confidentiality</li>
<li>Lack of privacy</li>
<li>Staff using adolescent clients as bad example</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="health-facility-barriers">Health facility barriers<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#health-facility-barriers" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Not designed to cater for youth (Inappropriate opening hours, long waiting time)</li>
<li>Lack of youth friendly corners</li>
<li>Cost of RH services</li>
<li>Availability of RH services</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="socio-cultural-barriers">Socio-cultural barriers<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#socio-cultural-barriers" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Lack/inadequate information about youth friendly services among community members</li>
<li>Community beliefs, attitudes and misconceptions</li>
<li>Community cultural and religious beliefs</li>
<li>Level of education</li>
<li>Political environment</li>
</ul>
<p>Reproductive health Lecture notes. Rugendo.M.M @2018 Kabarnet KMTC</p>
<p>Reproductive health Lecture notes. Rugendo.M.M @2018 Kabarnet KMTC</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="adolescent-barriers">Adolescent barriers<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#adolescent-barriers" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>&gt; Being embarrassed
&gt; Fear of Medical procedures (blood tests, pelvic exam)
Non-friendly service providers
&gt; Negative perceived notions towards service providers
&gt; Service provider's attitudes to SRH problems
&gt; Stigma associated with sexual activity and sexual health problems
&gt; Fear of discussing ARH problems with adults
&gt; Lack of awareness of risks/symptoms of SRH problems
&gt; Unaware of location of SRH facility and services offered
&gt; Fear of facilities with mixed clientele
&gt; Dislike seeking services within their locality</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="patterns-of-seeking-reproductive-health-services-by-adolescents">Patterns of seeking Reproductive Health services by adolescents<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#patterns-of-seeking-reproductive-health-services-by-adolescents" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>&gt; Adolescents are late/poor seekers of SRH services
&gt; Adolescents camouflage SRH problems
&gt; Self-medication/treatment before seeking appropriate care e.g. for management of STIs, termination of pregnancy
&gt; Adolescents don't like to be seen seeking RH services
&gt; Adolescents tend to prefer seeking RH services at specific times eg after when other people have left the facility
&gt; Douching after sex with water/detergents to prevent pregnancy/STIs
&gt; Attempted abortions before carrying pregnancy to term</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="approaches-for-delivery-of-youth-friendly-services">Approaches for Delivery of Youth Friendly Services<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#approaches-for-delivery-of-youth-friendly-services" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>There are two approaches to provision of youth friendly services, namely:</p>
<ol>
<li>Targeted approach</li>
<li>Integrated approach</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="1-targeted-approach">1. Targeted approach<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#1-targeted-approach" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Services are designed and planned for youth alone.</li>
<li>Services maybe clinical, non-clinical or a combination of both.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="2-integrated-approach">2. Integrated approach<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#2-integrated-approach" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Young people receive services as part of the general public.</li>
<li>Special arrangements are made to make the services more acceptable to young people.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="models-applied-in-youth-friendly-services">Models applied in youth friendly services<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#models-applied-in-youth-friendly-services" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>They are three models to youth friendly services:</p>
<ol>
<li>Clinic based model</li>
<li>Youth centre model</li>
<li>School based model/peer programs</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="1-clinic-model">1. Clinic model<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#1-clinic-model" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>In this model, services are provided in a health facility.
The following services are Provided in this model: -</p>
<p>&gt; General Counseling Services.
&gt; Screening and treatment of Sexually transmitted infections, HIV/AIDS.
&gt; Voluntary Counseling and Testing (VCT)
&gt; Provision of information and Education on Reproductive Health.
&gt; Training in life skills.
&gt; Provision of post abortion care services.
&gt; Availability of IEC, audio / vision Materials.
&gt; Ante and post-natal care.
&gt; Comprehensives post rape care.
&gt; Provision of contraceptives including condoms.
&gt; Curative services for minor illness including ante &amp; postnatal care
&gt; Promoting community based and school based outreach / peer education activities.
&gt; Recreational facilities (Indoor and Outdoor) where possible.
&gt; Linkage to school based and Youth center based model
&gt; Referral where necessary</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="2-youth-centre-model">2. Youth centre model<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#2-youth-centre-model" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>In this model, services are provided in centres designated for youth friendly services where youths are likely to congregate. Mainly at market places, churches etc.</p>
<p>Provide the following services: -</p>
<ul>
<li>Health prevention and promotion.</li>
<li>General counseling services.</li>
<li>Provision of information and education on reproductive health.</li>
<li>Training in livelihood / life / income generation activities (IGA)</li>
<li>Availability of IEC, audio / visual materials.</li>
<li>Promoting school based outreach IEC activities.</li>
<li>Promoting school based outreach IEC activities.</li>
<li>Working with peer youth educators.</li>
<li>Provision of contraceptive including condoms</li>
<li>Recreation facilities (In and Outdoor games)</li>
<li>Voluntary Counseling and Testing (VCT)</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="3-school-based-model-peer-programs">3. School based model/peer programs<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#3-school-based-model-peer-programs" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Services are provided in school's premises and focuses on adolescents and youths in learning institutions.</p>
<p>Provides the following services: -</p>
<ul>
<li>Skill training.</li>
<li>General counseling services.</li>
<li>Peer education</li>
<li>School health talks</li>
<li>Personal hygiene</li>
<li>Sexuality and grown up</li>
<li>Reproductive Health</li>
<li>STD and HIV-AIDS Prevention</li>
<li>Rape Prevention</li>
</ul>
<p>Reproductive health Lecture notes. Rugendo.M.M @2018 Kabarnet KMTC</p>
<p>&gt; Communication / skills Post rape care
&gt; Linkage to clinic-based and Youth center based model
&gt; Referral for treatment and management</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="characteristics-of-youth-friendly-services">Characteristics of Youth Friendly Services<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#characteristics-of-youth-friendly-services" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>&gt; Convenient Working hours/time
&gt; Convenient location
&gt; Availability of adequate, space that is separate and offers sufficient privacy.
&gt; Comfortable secure surroundings.
&gt; Specially trained Staff.
&gt; Respect for young people
&gt; Adequate time for client provider interactions.
&gt; Necessary referral mechanism should be available.
&gt; Wide range of services available (like one stop shop)
&gt; Educational materials available on site and to take away.
&gt; Community mobilization / gatekeepers involvement
&gt; Youth involvement</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="minimum-conditions-for-youth-friendly-services">Minimum Conditions for Youth Friendly Services<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#minimum-conditions-for-youth-friendly-services" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>&gt; Affordability and accessibility
&gt; Safe and basic range of services
&gt; Privacy and confidentiality
&gt; Provider competence/attitude
&gt; Quality and consistency
&gt; Reliability and sustainability
&gt; Trained healthcare providers
&gt; Inbuilt monitoring and evaluation system</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="addressing-barriers-to-reproductive-health-services-among-adolescents-and-youths">Addressing barriers to Reproductive Health services among adolescents and youths<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#addressing-barriers-to-reproductive-health-services-among-adolescents-and-youths" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>♦ Barriers to youth friendly services can be addressed through the following ways: -</p>
<p>&gt; Reassure the adolescent that it is normal to feel, Embarrassed, Afraid or Shy
&gt; Provide accurate, factual information on adolescent growth and development.
&gt; Create awareness on availability of ASRH services through media, campaigns, IEC etc.
&gt; Give information: -To enable adolescents recognize signs and symptoms of STIs and explain the need to seek services early
&gt; Reassure adolescents on privacy and confidentiality.
&gt; Sensitize the community on: -
&gt;   - Adolescent SRH needs
&gt;   - Consequences of SRH behavior</p>
<p>Reproductive health Lecture notes. Rugendo.M.M @2018 Kabarnet KMTC</p>
<ul>
<li>Implications of not managing ASRH needs</li>
<li>The need for community support</li>
</ul>
<p>&gt; Define role of parents in giving SRH information
&gt; Training of health care workers on youth friendly services
&gt; Ensuring availability of reproductive health services
&gt; Ensuring that reproductive health services are accessible and affordable.
&gt; Creating youth friendly corners
&gt; Appropriate and convenient working hours
&gt; Reducing waiting time
&gt; Positive attitude towards young people among health care workers
&gt; Conducting outreaches on RH services.
&gt; Use of youth seminars, conferences and other related programs to create awareness
&gt; Working with youth groups within the community.
&gt; Develop a comprehensive reproductive health package to address youth/adolescent issues through the provision of counseling and user friendly clinics
&gt; Promote responsible and healthy RH and sexual behavior of the youth through counseling and guidance
&gt; Sensitize leaders, programme managers, service providers, teachers, the community, adolescents and youths themselves, on the reproductive health needs and rights of adolescents and youths
&gt; Advocating the recognition of socioeconomic and reproductive health needs and rights of adolescents and the youth
&gt; Establishing an understanding with youth advisory councils at all levels to coordinate and advise on youth and adolescent health
&gt; Developing specific messages for different target groups (parents, religious and other leaders, youths and adolescents)
&gt; Implementing youth friendly and accessible RH services to enable the youth to seek services and receive counseling without barriers. Health providers should create a conducive environment when counseling and avoid biases that discourage youths from coming to the facility
&gt; Educating youths on their rights in order to help them attain the highest degree of health and self-esteem.
&gt; Conducting basic/applied research on youth and adolescent issues on regular basis and implementing the findings
&gt; Policy formulation on youth and adolescent issues regarding reproductive health.</p>
<p>Reproductive health Lecture notes. Rugendo.M.M @2018 Kabarnet KMTC</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="preconception-care">Preconception Care<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#preconception-care" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="learning-objectives">Learning objectives<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#learning-objectives" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>By the end of the lesson the learner should be able to: -</li>
</ul>
<ol>
<li>Define preconception care</li>
<li>Outline objectives of preconception care</li>
<li>Discuss importance of preconception care</li>
<li>To outline services provided in preconception care.</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="definition">Definition<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#definition" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>This is a set of interventions that identify and modify biomedical, behavioural, and social risks to a woman's health and future pregnancies. It includes health promotion, prevention and management of any preexisting conditions; emphasizing health issues that require action before conception or very early in pregnancy for maximal impact. The target population for pre conception care is women of reproductive age (15 to 49 years), although men are also targeted by several components of pre conception care.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="objectives-of-pre-conception-care">Objectives of Pre conception Care:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#objectives-of-pre-conception-care" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>To provide Health promotion and education to improve knowledge attitudes and behaviours of men and women with regard to pregnancy</li>
<li>To provide Evidence - based Screening for pregnancy risks</li>
<li>To provide Interventions to address identified risks and conditions</li>
<li>To Achieve universal coverage of Essential Obstetric Care</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="reasons-for-focusing-on-preconception-care-include">Reasons for focusing on preconception care include: -<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#reasons-for-focusing-on-preconception-care-include" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Poor birth outcomes continue</li>
<li>Increasing Newborn mortality rate.</li>
<li>Postpartum hemorrhage</li>
<li>Poor pregnancy outcomes e.g. malaria and anaemia remain prevalent; smoking, alcohol use and drug abuse are on the increase.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="reproductive-health-risks-include-the-following">Reproductive Health risks include the following:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#reproductive-health-risks-include-the-following" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Age of the couple</li>
<li>Very young (16yrs and below); Elderly (35 yrs and above)</li>
<li>Parity</li>
<li>Primigravida; Grand multiparity (gravida five and above); Short pregnancy interval (less than 2 years)</li>
<li>Nutritional status</li>
<li>Under nutrition, obesity, malnutrition</li>
<li>Low Socio-economic status</li>
<li>Previous adverse pregnancy outcome</li>
<li>Recurrent spontaneous abortions, Stillbirths, Early neonatal deaths (first one week)</li>
</ul>
<p>Reproductive health Lecture notes. Rugendo.M.M @2018 Kabarnet KMTC</p>
<ul>
<li>Previous baby with congenital abnormalities</li>
<li>Medical conditions such as</li>
<li>Anaemia, Malaria, HIV/AIDS, Tuberculosis, STIs/RTIs, cardiac disease, Diabetes, Sickle cell disease, Asthma, Hypertension (Pre and post conception) ABO and Rhesus incompatibility, Breast cancer, cervical cancer, renal disease</li>
<li>Obstetric Complications such as</li>
<li>Previous obstetric Haemorrhage; previous C/S scars, previous preterm labour, Previous PET / eclampsia</li>
<li>Substance abuse</li>
<li>Smoking; Alcohol or Drug abuse; Intake of prescription or over the counter drugs that are known to be teratogens.</li>
<li>Gender based violence</li>
<li>FGM, Early marriage, Physical / psychological abuse, Sexual violence</li>
<li>Negative cultural practices</li>
<li>Food restrictions, Health seeking behavior</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="preconception-care-protocol">Preconception care protocol<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#preconception-care-protocol" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>&gt; History taking should be comprehensive and include</p>
<ul>
<li>Family history: hereditary conditions, Medical conditions, congenital abnormalities</li>
<li>Medical history: Diabetes, hypertension, HIV, TB, RT cancers e.g. Breast cancer, cervical cancer</li>
<li>Surgical history: Previous myomectomy, C/section, Obstetric fistula repair</li>
<li>Obstetric/gynecological history: Pregnancy wastage, previous preterm deliveries, STI/RTI, menstrual disorders, prolonged sub fertility</li>
<li>Environmental history: exposure to radiation, Chemical</li>
<li>Occupational history: type of work and length of working hours as in long distance drivers, athletes, bicycle riders</li>
<li>Nutritional history: diet</li>
<li>Male partner history: mumps, STIs/HIV, substance abuse, tight clothing (around scrotum)</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="physical-examination">Physical examination<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#physical-examination" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>This should encompass a general examination (head to toe) to include vital signs, weight; e.t.c.</li>
<li>The systemic examination of the thyroid, heart, breasts, abdomen, pelvis and other relevant systems will be based on the history obtained from the woman.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="investigations">Investigations<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#investigations" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Minimum investigations should include: Full blood count, random blood sugar, Syphilis test, HIV test, Blood group and rhesus, Urinalysis</li>
<li>Additional investigations are based on the history and examination</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="interventions">Interventions:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#interventions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Health education and counselling</li>
</ul>
<p>Reproductive health Lecture notes. Rugendo.M.M @2018 Kabarnet KMTC</p>
<p><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Psychosocial counselling
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Family planning: Each woman, man, and couple should be encouraged to have a reproductive life plan including healthy timing and spacing of pregnancy
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Life styles issues
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Nutrition: Assess dietary status and advice on healthy nutrition.
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Weight: Check BMI, advise on weight gain or loss where BMI in &lt;20 or &gt;30
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Substance abuse such as alcohol, hard drugs, tobacco, traditional medications, herbs
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Timing of intercourse: Check that the couple understands the ovulatory cycle and can determine the most fertile days relative to the woman's cycle. Advice that for conception to occur, intercourse should occur regularly (two to three times a week and should cover the most fertile time.)
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Regular exercises
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Adequate rest
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Spiritual nourishment
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Prenatal diagnosis: Educate women about options for prenatal diagnosis including genetic counseling (Down's syndrome, sickle cell disease, thalassemia, medical conditions); and virologic screening (TORCHES)
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Discourage over the counter drugs and use of teratogenic medications</p>
<ul>
<li>Other Specific interventions
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Prophylaxis
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Folic Acid
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Women who are trying to conceive should take folic acid supplements (400mcg) daily to reduce the risk of neural tube defects. This should begin 3months before pregnancy. Women with a history of neural tube defects or epilepsy should take 5mg daily.
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Iron, Zinc, Vitamin A 10,000 IU, Iodine and Calcium may be taken during the preconception period depending on the health status of the patient and any underlying medical conditions or risks.
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Management of Pre-existing medical problems
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Stabilize medical conditions and ensure that medical control is optimal
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Check that any drugs or treatments used are safe for use in pregnancy and do not affect sperm function (cytotoxic and radiation, smoking and alcohol etc)
<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">✓</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\checkmark</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">✓</span></span></span></span></span> Where appropriate, refer women for specialized care.</li>
</ul>
<p><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo>⋄</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\diamond</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.4445em;"></span><span class="mord">⋄</span></span></span></span></span> Nutrition in the pre-conception period</p>
<ul>
<li>Pre-pregnancy nutrition is as important as nutrition during pregnancy.</li>
</ul>
<p>Reproductive health Lecture notes. Rugendo.M.M @2018 Kabarnet KMTC</p>
<ul>
<li>It influences a woman's ability to conceive, determines the foetal growth and development and as such the size of the foetus and its overall health as well as the health of the mother.</li>
<li>A woman's body provides the environment for conception and development of the foetus; therefore, her nutrition influences the health of that environment.</li>
<li>A well-nourished woman before conception begins her pregnancy with a reserve of several nutrients so that the needs of the foetus can be met without jeopardizing her health.</li>
<li>Underweight and overweight women experience more complications during pregnancy than normal women.</li>
<li>Underweight women risk delivering preterm and low birth weight infants. Obese women have an increased risk of complications such as hypertension, gestational diabetes and higher risk of caesarean sections since they tend to deliver larger birth weight babies.</li>
<li>Low birth weight (LBW) is a major underlying cause of infant mortality and other developmental and learning disorders in children.</li>
<li>Full term infants weighing less than 2500 grams are referred to as small for gestational age (SGA) and this is due to intrauterine growth retardation (IUGR). Deficiencies of some nutrients such as calcium, iron, vitamin D and folic acid as well as the use of certain drugs and alcohol have detrimental effects embryonic growth even before a woman realizes she is pregnant.</li>
<li>Pre-pregnancy BMI influences gestational weight gain and favorable pregnancy outcome. It is recommended that more emphasis be placed on preconception and early pregnancy nutrition due to the following reasons:</li>
<li>In Kenya, 17-18% of all births are to women under the age of 20 years. This is a time of rapid physical growth with nutritional requirements increasing significantly to support growth and development. The additional energy and nutrient demands of pregnancy place adolescents at nutritional risk.</li>
<li>Prevention of stunting in girl children during the first two years can help break the cycle of malnutrition and improves their chances of surviving the delivery. Stunted women are at risk of obstructed labour because of the disproportion between the size of the baby's head and the maternal pelvis.</li>
<li>Approximately 50% of cases of neural tube defects may be prevented with adequate intakes of folic acid from the pre-conception period and throughout the early months of pregnancy.</li>
<li>Birth weight is closely associated with child survival, well-being, and growth. Nutrient stores built up in adolescence determine the nutrition of the mother when she enters pregnancy during and between pregnancies. This in turn impacts on birth weight and child survival.</li>
<li>Efforts to improve eating patterns and achieve healthy weights can be implemented, in part, through school-based nutrition programs and integration of nutrition and health promotion counselling into primary health care services.</li>
</ul>
<p>Reproductive health Lecture notes. Rugendo.M.M @2018 Kabarnet KMTC</p>
